     <div class="sidebar-widget slider" id="facts">
      <div class="header">
       <h5>
        <a href="/israel-facts/">
         Did You Know?
        </a>
       </h5>
       <h6>
        <a href="/israel-facts/">
         Facts From Israel
        </a>
       </h6>
      </div>
      <div class="arrow-prev">
       <a class="buttons prev disabled" href="#" title="Next Fact">
       </a>
      </div>
      <div id="facts-viewport">
       <ul>
        <li class="item slide1">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Technology
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          An Israeli-developed alogrithm enabled NASA to transmit images from Mars.
         </div>
        </li>
        <li class="item slide2">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Health
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          The success of GlaxoSmithKline’s once-a-day breast cancer pill Tykerb – which has won approval by the FDA for use by women with metastatic or advanced breast cancer – is thanks in part to clinical trials conducted by Israeli researchers.
         </div>
        </li>
        <li class="item slide3">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Technology
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          <a href="https://www.israel21c.org/the-wild-tale-behind-your-pet-hamster/" target="_blank">
           All pet Syrian hamsters
          </a>
          are descendants of a family brought to Jerusalem 86 years ago by Israel's first Hebrew zoologist.
         </div>
        </li>
        <li class="item slide4">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Health
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          Israeli microbiologists have developed the first passive vaccine against the mosquito-borne West Nile virus.
         </div>
        </li>
        <li class="item slide5">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Health
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          An Israeli has invented a ‘bone glue’ that will reduce the need for bone transplants and heal bone defects caused by cancer.
         </div>
        </li>
        <li class="item slide6">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Health
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          An Israeli company has developed a revolutionary new tool that could allow surgeons to close wounds
          <a href="https://www.israel21c.org/health/say-goodbye-to-surgical-stitches-and-staples/" target="_blank">
           without stitches or staples
          </a>
          minimalizing scarring and risk of infection.
         </div>
        </li>
        <li class="item slide7">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Technology
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          Israeli mini-unmanned aerial vehicles are being used by US forces in Iraq and Afghanistan.
         </div>
        </li>
        <li class="item slide8">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Technology
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          Israel is ranked #2 in the world for venture capital funds right behind the US.
         </div>
        </li>
        <li class="item slide9">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Health
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          Israeli researchers believe they may have found a way to
          <a href="https://www.israel21c.org/health/israelis-find-way-to-preserve-fertility-after-chemotherapy/" target="_blank">
           preserve the fertility of young female cancer patients
          </a>
          undergoing chemotherapy.
         </div>
        </li>
        <li class="item slide10">
         <div class="hashtag">
          #Environment
         </div>
         <div class="content">
          An Israeli company has developed
          <a href="https://www.israel21c.org/the-top-12-ways-israel-feeds-the-world/">
           reusable plastic trays to collect dew from the air
          </a>
          , reducing the water needed by crops or trees by up to 50 percent.
         </div>
        </li>
       </ul>
      </div>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   jQuery("document").ready(function(){
			var uncover_israel_poped = 0;
			jQuery(".popup_darker .close_btn").click(function(){
				jQuery(".popup_darker").fadeOut(200);
			});

			jQuery(window).scroll(function(e) {
				if(!uncover_israel_poped && in_scroll("#headlines") && !rgb_get_cookie("uncoverilpop")){
					uncover_israel_poped = 1;
					jQuery("#uncover_israel_popup").fadeIn(600);
					rgb_set_cookie("uncoverilpop",1,30);
				}
			});


		});
  </script>
